function ck_sess_connect()
{
$.ajax({
url: 'ck_sess_connect.php',
data: {
},
type : 'POST',
timeout: 30000,
success: function(txt){
if (txt=='1'){
return true;
}else{
location.replace(window.location.href.replace('#',''));
}
},
error: function(){
location.replace(window.location.href.replace('#',''));
}
});
}

function cancella_firma(){
var conf=false;
if( $("#firmaparziale").is(':checked') == true){
// al momento non faccio niente
conf=confirm("Vuoi aggiungere una firma?");
}
else{

conf=false;
alert("Non è possibile sovrascrivere un'ora firmata");



}
return conf;
};

$('#scritta_tim').click( function() {
if($(this).attr('stato') == 'P'){
$(this).attr('stato','M');
$("#scritta_tim").html("mostra stato");
$(".tim_desc_mensa").show();
$(".tim_desc_stato").hide();
}
else{
$(this).attr('stato','P');
$("#scritta_tim").html("mostra mensa");
$(".tim_desc_mensa").hide();
$(".tim_desc_stato").show();
}

})

$(document).keydown(function(e)
{
var el = document.activeElement;

if(el.hasAttribute('tab_item_for') && (e.which == 13 || (e.which == 32 && !$(el).is("input") && !$(el).is("textarea"))))
{
if(el.tagName !== 'SELECT')
{
e.preventDefault();
e.stopPropagation();
}

var event_el = ($(el).attr('tab_item_for') == 'this') ? el : $(el).attr('tab_item_for');

$(event_el).focus();
$(event_el).click();
}
});

});
